    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yes, but each book is a complete standalone with different characters. The connecting factor with the four novels in the series is each book is based <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yes, but each book is a complete standalone with different characters. The connecting factor with the four novels in the series is each book is based off of one of the four elements: air, water, earth, and fire. :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_1400812329" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400812329" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1400812329?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=grief">grief</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1400812329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13753275987818563473"><b>3 Stars<br/><br/>***UNPOPULAR OPINION ALERT***</b><br/><br/><i>***Disclaimer***</i><br/>A lot of people say "I was able to overlook a, b, and c about the book and enjoy it" and "it's still on my tbr," and that's great. I'm not trying to disuade people from reading this. It <i>should</i> be on people's tbr because it's a great book. <br/><br/>And I'm glad others are overlooking certain things and loving it. I could have very well done the same. But I chose not to because that's just my true opinion. So please don't see my review as me not being abl</span>
  <span id="freeText13753275987818563473" style="display:none"><b>3 Stars<br><br>***UNPOPULAR OPINION ALERT***</b><br><br><i>***Disclaimer***</i><br>A lot of people say "I was able to overlook a, b, and c about the book and enjoy it" and "it's still on my tbr," and that's great. I'm not trying to disuade people from reading this. It <i>should</i> be on people's tbr because it's a great book. <br><br>And I'm glad others are overlooking certain things and loving it. I could have very well done the same. But I chose not to because that's just my true opinion. So please don't see my review as me not being able to "rise above" and see the good because that's not the case. And I'm not trying to compel others to do the same or not read this book. The below is simply MY opinion...<br><br><b>Don't stab me, brah.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443349124ra/16351625.gif" width="483.75" height="271.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>So I know a lot of you might be thinking that cold-hearted, soulless Val once again just couldn't see past the <s>sappiness</s> sweetness to truly <i>appreciate</i> the <i>poignancy</i> here...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443349124i/16351626._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="359.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...or that maybe I just don't understand pain and grief.<br><br>Well, rest assured, that's not the case. <br><br>Cause I've been there.<br><br>And it's the worst fucking thing in the world, as I'm sure a lot of people here know and relate to.<br><br>But anysadz, I'm not one of those folks who like to repeatedly pick at my own scabs...which is actually why I typically avoid reading books like this one. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443349124i/16351627._SX540_.jpg" width="612" height="511" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because why remind yourself of some of your worst memories under the guise of "fun" reading, amiright?<br><br>However, in this case, I only read the blurb and not actual reviews of the book. All I saw was a shitload of 5-star reviews so I picked it up not realizing it dealt with certain topics I typically and unfailingly avoid. <br><br>That said, I really enjoyed this book. <br><br>Yes, you read that right. <br><br>The author did a really great job with these two severely broken characters. <br><br>The way they expressed their pain to each other? <br><br>The words they used to describe it?<br><br>The fucking feathers?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443350145ra/16351721.gif" width="400" height="194" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So heartfelt and so well done.<br><br><b>In fact, I was ready to smack 5 stars on this bad boy and wax poetic in my review.</b><br><br>*<br>*<br>*<br><br><b>Until about the 80% mark.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443350822ra/16351760.gif" width="350" height="197" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And then shit just seem to come off the rails a bit. <br><br>Things started to get rushed...<br><br>Some twists I had suspected early on started to unfold with a few too many "coincidences" to keep grounded in "realistic land" and propelled it straight into Days of Our Lives land...<br><br>A few other eye-roll-worthy 90210 style shenanigans ensued...<br><br>And then Tristan's behavior suddenly flew high and right. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443350822ra/16351761.gif" width="600" height="373" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall I just wanted this book to be longer.<br><br>As I said, I think the first 80% was great. <br><br>But I felt like instead of building on the foundation created in that first 80% - the progress Elizabeth and Tristan experienced both individually and as a unit - and THEN getting to the twists and turns, there was just a sense of "okay, good enough, now let's get to the end."<br><br>In fact, it was so abrupt and flagging that the last 20% dropped me down from an I'm-fucking-loving-this-5-star to a minus-2-what-the-fuck-just-happened-stars. <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443351378ra/16351780.gif" width="320" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Keep in mind I am DEFINITELY in the minority on this one. <br><br>There really IS a lot to love about this book - It's a great story and it's very well-written<br><br>However, there was just one too many holes in the yacht floor for me. <br><br>Find me at:<br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477498810i/20958471.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477498810i/20958472.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

</a><br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br>Okay, this ish has been blowing the fuck outta my feed with all my friends' 5 star reviews. <br><br>And when all of your friends jump off a cliff...<br><br>There is now a layer of <s>bodies</s> cushioning down there to land on...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427814410ra/14323606.gif" width="245" height="311" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jay Kay, Jaaaaay Kay. <br><br>If all my peeps say this is awesome, I want to play too!</span>

<div id="review_1370257437" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1370257437" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1370257437?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=beta-read">beta-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1370257437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7711481722086619915"><b>5++ stars!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807757._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>The Air He Breathes</i> is the most beautiful book I’ve read this year. It’s a stunning, emotional, heartbreaking and powerful read. It’s outstanding and it’s by far Brittainy’s best work and my favorite book of hers. In fact, it’s my favorite book of 2015. Yes. You read that right. The same author that wrote my favorite book of 2014 (Loving Mr. Daniels) also wrote my favorite book of 2015. This is a book that will stay with you and one you don’t want to miss out on reading. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807758._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Loss.</b> It can</span>
  <span id="freeText7711481722086619915" style="display:none"><b>5++ stars!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807757._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>The Air He Breathes</i> is the most beautiful book I’ve read this year. It’s a stunning, emotional, heartbreaking and powerful read. It’s outstanding and it’s by far Brittainy’s best work and my favorite book of hers. In fact, it’s my favorite book of 2015. Yes. You read that right. The same author that wrote my favorite book of 2014 (Loving Mr. Daniels) also wrote my favorite book of 2015. This is a book that will stay with you and one you don’t want to miss out on reading. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807758._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Loss.</b> It can be devastating and debilitating. Losing someone you love has to be one of the worst feelings in the world. Losing the love of your life makes it that much worse. Elizabeth is trying her best to move on, to live every day. To breathe. It helps that she has Emma, her beautiful daughter. She has to stay strong. For her. After an extended visit with her Mama, Elizabeth decides to come home. It’s time. When she gets there, things around her are much of the same, but nothing feels the same for her. <br><br>Then she meets him. The new town jerk. The guy everyone talks about but avoids. Tristan Cole. <br><b>
  <blockquote>People in town called him an asshole, and I could see why. He wasn’t nice, he wasn’t stable, and he was broken in all of the wrong and right places.</blockquote>
</b> <br>There is more than Tristan than meets the eye. You know that loss we talked about earlier? Tristan has had the ultimate loss. And it forever changed him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807759._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The last thing Tristan Cole wants is a friend. But Elizabeth befriends him anyway. He resists, but eventually, she wears him down. Her persistence is stronger then his stubbornness. For the first time since his loss, Tristan finds some happiness and even a little peace with Elizabeth and Emma. They are bonded together by their loss. Their loss is what connects them at first. It’s clear as day they are attracted to one another, though both are hesitant to act on it. The progression of their relationship is paced perfectly. They are both damaged, but together, they feel a little more whole. Even if it only is pretend… for now. <br><i>
  <blockquote>He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.</blockquote>
</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807760._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I wasn’t him. She wasn’t her. But my God, it felt good to lie to ourselves. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br>Lets talk about the characters- Tristan was such a jerk at the beginning. I wasn’t sure he would win me over, but he certainly did. I loved that even when he and Liz’s friendship started to grow, he didn’t automatically change. It was a gradual progression and it worked well with the story. You could tell how hurt and damaged he was and it took a lot of time for him to come around. And a ton of patience on Liz’s part. <br><br>Lizzie was just amazing. She was such a strong heroine. She lost so much, yet was able to give so much of herself to helping Tristan and accepting him. I love that she didn’t care what others thought of her being friends with him etc. I loved the kind of mother she was to Emma and also what kind of friend she was. She had great character. And a special shout out to her best friend- seriously what a hoot! Faye brought some much needed laughter to the serious story and was a great addition.<br><br>Another thing I loved about this book is that it wasn’t predictable. There were several twists I didn’t see coming at all. I love being surprised in a book. I also loved so much how the friendship turned into something more. At first it started just as a way for the two of them to cope, then it turned into something beautiful. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807761._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Brittainy C Cherry can tell a story like no other. She has this way of sucking you in with her endearing tales, lovable characters and flawless writing. She is like a unicorn. That one special author that never fails to produce a book that goes straight to the top of my favorites list. The one who writes and speaks to my heart, my mind and my soul. <br><br>If you’re looking for a book that will make you feel, make you love, move you and make your heart soar, read this book. I cried, I smiled, I cried some more, and by the end, I may have cried again (those were the happy tears). I highlighted a ton because every page was stunning. Every scene had something worth highlighting. The lines in this book were beyond gorgeous. <br><br><i>The Air He Breathes</i> is the most beautiful story of love, loss, friendship, healing and perseverance. It’s a book that is sitting at #1 on my favorites list and one I would recommend to any and everyone. I’m shouting it from the rooftops here <b>READ THIS BOOK!</b> You won’t regret it! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504723086i/23807762._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*I had the pleasure of beta reading this beautiful story for the lovely Brittainy C Cherry</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7711481722086619915" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1401474160" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1401474160" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1401474160?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/29854191-the-air-he-breathes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1401474160" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8269326903496127807">Wow! This was a highly emotional, and often depressing, story. Despite the fact that it dealt with some pretty gloomy subject matter, I was completely hooked on this story. I listened to the Audible version and I finished it in a single day. I couldn't pull myself away from it.<br/><br/>The author doesn't waste any time before plunging you into the desolate lives of Elizabeth and Tristan. Both of them are broken, trying to make it through their lives one day at a time. Elizabeth has lost her husband and i</span>
  <span id="freeText8269326903496127807" style="display:none">Wow! This was a highly emotional, and often depressing, story. Despite the fact that it dealt with some pretty gloomy subject matter, I was completely hooked on this story. I listened to the Audible version and I finished it in a single day. I couldn't pull myself away from it.<br /><br />The author doesn't waste any time before plunging you into the desolate lives of Elizabeth and Tristan. Both of them are broken, trying to make it through their lives one day at a time. Elizabeth has lost her husband and is struggling to hold it together for her young daughter. Tristan can't move past the loss of his wife and son, becoming an antisocial recluse and the topic of town gossip.<br /><br />A twist of fate has these two crossing paths when Elizabeth hits Tristan's dog with her car by accident. To say that Tristan is an ass, is putting it mildly. He is a pretty despicable person in the beginning.<br /><br />As Elizabeth begins to peel back the layers, she sees far more than either of them had ever expected. She can see the pain that he hides with his gruff demeanor. She recognizes that he is afraid to get close to anyone, only to risk losing them again. She knows all of the signs, because she's feeling the same pain.<br /><br />Gradually, Tristan warms up to Elizabeth and we get glimpses of the man he is inside. The two begin a "friends with benefits" relationship that soon morphs into much more. Along the way, I fell in love with Tristan. Of course, I loved Elizabeth from the get go. <br /><br />Just when things are going perfectly, Ms. Cherry drops a bomb. Honestly, I kind of saw it coming. However, whether you figure out the twist or not, it will wreck your world. I was so heartbroken for these two, which was followed shortly by anger and outrage.<br /><br />Up to that point, I was thinking this would be a five-star read for me. I was an emotional mess, but in the way that can only be achieved by reading a really great story. It was beautiful.<br /><br />Then, the story took a turn for the worse. After the first big reveal, the secrets and twists started coming out of everywhere. For me, the story went from heartfelt to far-fetched and unbelievable. It was like the author couldn't decide which way to take the story, so she threw in everything that had crossed her mind and tried to wrap it up in a few short chapters. <br /><br />Up until about 85-90% I was in love with this book. Then, it kind of got a little unnecessarily dramatic and lost some of it's appeal for me. However, even with the over the top ending, I really enjoyed this book. <br /><br />It was still a fantastic story and I'm so glad I finally got around to it. Sometime soon, I hope to et to the second book in this series. I'm just taking a few days to get my emotions in check again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8269326903496127807" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1457175391" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1457175391" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1457175391?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26721257-the-air-he-breathes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=alternative-pov">alternative-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=terrible">terrible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=cringeworthy">cringeworthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=go-straight-into-the-wall">go-straight-into-the-wall</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=masochist-me">masochist-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=what-is-your-point">what-is-your-point</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=authors-i-will-never-read-again">authors-i-will-never-read-again</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1457175391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17555724014085133541"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Edit</u>
</b> : Here's my romance scale, with the points that interest <i>me</i> (tell me if you think of something else^^)<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449228815i/17254120._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Warning</u>
</b> : <b>This is a DNF review of a book I pretty much hated</b>. As much as I would have wanted to finish it, I reached 34% and there's no redeeming this book.<br/><br/>Just a little over a year ago, I started reviewing books on Goodreads. I gave up on New Adult at roughly the same time. Well, more or less, and this is why : <br/>- They often romanticize unhealthy/abusive relationships and are full </span>
  <span id="freeText17555724014085133541" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Edit</u>
</b> : Here's my romance scale, with the points that interest <i>me</i> (tell me if you think of something else^^)<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449228815i/17254120._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Warning</u>
</b> : <b>This is a DNF review of a book I pretty much hated</b>. As much as I would have wanted to finish it, I reached 34% and there's no redeeming this book.<br><br>Just a little over a year ago, I started reviewing books on Goodreads. I gave up on New Adult at roughly the same time. Well, more or less, and this is why : <br>- They often romanticize unhealthy/abusive relationships and are full of sexist tropes.<br>- Honestly, most of them <b>aren't</b> well-written.<br>- They rely on unrealistic and over the top drama. <br><br>So, yes. A few of them are good, and when I stumbled across <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564446.The_Air_He_Breathes__Elements___1_" title="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Air He Breathes</a>, I decided to try it because <b>a)</b> Did you see the ridiculously high rating? <b>b) </b>It was part of the Romance Finalists in the Goodreads Choice Awards and <b>c)</b> It was a freebie. That blurb, though. I'm not gonna lie, it screamed cheap NA to me, but I know I can be judgmental towards blurbs so I didn't listen to my instincts. <br><br><b><u>Verdict</u> : I should have trusted my guts, because this book is TERRIBLE</b>, and if I usually understand why people love books I personally hate, <u>I just can't here</u>. Poorly written, following a ridiculous storyline filled with clichés and stereotypes &amp; punctuated by cringing dialogues. <br><br>This leads me to : <b>WHAT THE FUCK DID I JUST READ?</b><br><br>The story starts with the two main characters relating the deaths of their loved-ones. <b>Four</b>, to be exact, because life is a bitch in NA, you know. What better way to picture characters who are BROKEN than let them shattered by the deaths of their respective significant others? Oh, I know : add a child's death (because tears. Tears are always good for sells) and a father's death, too, just for the sake of having the female-lead say things like, <br><br><i>"Mama became a whore after Dad died. (...) There weren't many other ways to put it other than that."</i> <br><br>I personally could find other ways to say that your mother dates a lot, but hey, maybe that's just me. Don't be too worried though! She's sure her mum never cheated on her father before his death, because <i>"when he'd go off to work at the crack of dawn, she would have his breakfast and lunch packed with snacks"</i>. <br><br>So, just tell me if I misunderstood, girl, but you're either a whore or a housewife. Nice. (3%, and I already knew our relationship wouldn't be easy, UGH)<br><br><b>But moving on</b>. <br><br>Because with four deaths we didn't reach the end of our NA drama feast (WOOT!), <b>Liz hits a dog with her car</b>. And then you think, she is a decent human being, I guess? She's going to take care of him, surely? Yes she does, but before checking on the poor dog LYING ON THE GROUND, she takes the time to <b>a)</b> stare fixedly into the eyes of the owner that <i>"match the shadows of the sky right before a thunderstorm"</i> (whatever that means), <b>b) </b>notice his clothes, his headphones, his muscular arms, his fucking (absence of) SHOES, <b>all of this before looking at the poor dog LYING ON THE GROUND</b>. I mean, okay. Psycho much? Unsurprisingly Tristan (of course he's our love interest!) is pretty pissed and sort of yell at her right away. <br><br>About this : the only criticism I've read about this book is the way Tristan acts when they meet. Let me get this straight : I don't condone any kind of violence, even verbal, BUT SHE JUST HIT HIS DOG WITH HER CAR AND IS STARING AT HIM LIKE A DROOLING FANGIRL. Trust me, I would be beyond pissed if someone hit my dog, and I'm not a yelling kind of person. <br><br><b>But moving on</b>. <br><br>That's when I realized that this kind of book turned me into a psycho : they're at the vet, and kind of bicker all the way - not in a love/hate banter fashion, mind you, but more like this : <br><br><i>"Are you always... always..."<br>"Always what? Spit it out! Use words!" he ordered.</i><br><br>So charming, right?<br><br>So, they're at the vet. Poor dog is healed. And then, there's this (Liz is describing): <br><br><i>"He lost himself in his emotions, and when he exhaled, he began to sob uncontrollably. He wailed, his tears harsh, raw, and painful."</i><br><br>I laughed at that. I'm a terrible human being. <br><br><b>But moving on</b>. <br><br>Because <b>a NA wouldn't be a NA without some kind of woman hating, Liz encounters her old neighbors who - OF COURSE - are the perfect stereotypes of noisy, mean and gossip women</b>. Of course Liz hates every second of their conversation. They complain about the poor state of her yard and say stuff like this : <i>"After Stephen died, you left so fast that I wasn't able to make you any comfort food, so now I was finally able to make you this meatloaf to help you mourn"</i> or this : <i>"But, just to be clear, Emma [her little daughter] is not suffering from depression, is she? I hear that can be quite contagious with other kids."</i> Because women are all kinds of stupid aren't they? ARGG. <br><br>Oh, by the way, thanks for the *discreet* info-dumping beautifully hidden in the dialogues. *snorts*<br><br>Speaking of women, <b>let's talk about her best friend, okay?</b> See, I'm always happy when authors picture women who have an active sex-life without slut-shaming them, so at first I thought, hey, good. I was a fool. There's a stereotype I hate almost as much : <b>the crazy, over-the-top best-friend whose sex-life is never directly condemned but discreetly mocked</b>. <br><br>Meet Faye. Faye is happy.<br><br> <i>"[she] snuggled her head against my breasts, as if they were her pillow."</i><br><br>Faye is 27. <br><br>Faye doesn't know that a (bad) joke is always better told only <b>once</b>. <br><br><i>"Or, you could fire Sam," Faye offered. "He already has another part-time job! Plus, he's kind of creepy."<br>"I can hear you," Sam said, shyly."</i> (she's going to make that joke third times)<br><br>Faye has no filters. <br><br><i>"What do you mean you're trying to get laid?" I gasped. "Faye, are you having sex right now?"<br>(...)<br>"Well, if you mean is there a penis currently sitting in my vagina, then yes. I guess you could semi call that sex."<br>"Oh my God, Faye! Why the hell would you answer the phone?!"<br>"Um, because chicks before dicks? Like, literally." <b>She laughed. I gagged</b>."</i><br><br>Let's pay a little attention at what we're being sold, okay? <b>Faye, the sexually active best-friend, is annoying and unbearable</b>. She talks (loudly) about Liz's "aging" vagina while Liz is serving customers at the restaurant. She visits at night with friends after Liz explicitly texted her that she was fine (don't mind me on this, apparently that's okay - I'm certainly awkward to find that annoying). <b>Truth is, it's sneaky, but I felt as if this ridiculous stereotype of a woman's purpose was to make us despise her, and with her, women who date</b> (the mother is a whore, remember?). <br><br><b><u>This is what the book is telling us</u> (in my opinion) : <i>So, women, you want to have a sex-life? Don't you see how ridiculous you would be?</i></b><br><br>Fuck you, book. <br><br><b>But moving on</b>. <br><br>I'm sure that by this point <b>you're dying to know how the romance between our two *insert gagging emoji* broken souls will unfold</b>. <br><br>Well, you know, <b>the usual</b> : <br><br>fighting ► <b>forced kiss</b> ► <i>OMG this is HAWT!</i> ► pushing away. <br><br>ARGG. <b>Terrible book, not recommended</b>. <br><a title="Twitter" href="https://twitter.com/A_Starcrossed" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467543123i/19603102._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://meetthebookworld.com/reviews-3/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="http://www.facebook.com/meetthebookworld/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487853349i/22057439.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="http://meetthebookworld.com/contact/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487853349i/22057440.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1350752705" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1350752705" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1350752705?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1350752705" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9172019294531054932"><b>5 + STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"How did two people so broken find each other's shattered pieces?"</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span> <br/><br/>This book is so much more than it's gorgeous cover! I highly advise one-click purchasing because Britainy C. Cherry has delivered one of my favorite reads of 2015!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Show me the shadows that keep you up at night. Kiss me with your darkness."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Ms. Cherry’s writing was simply fantastic, while her characters popped right off damn the page. I’m still reeling from the array of emotions that this </span>
  <span id="freeText9172019294531054932" style="display:none"><b>5 + STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>"How did two people so broken find each other's shattered pieces?"</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>This book is so much more than it's gorgeous cover! I highly advise one-click purchasing because Britainy C. Cherry has delivered one of my favorite reads of 2015!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Show me the shadows that keep you up at night. Kiss me with your darkness."</i>
</b><br><br>Ms. Cherry’s writing was simply fantastic, while her characters popped right off damn the page. I’m still reeling from the array of emotions that this story packed. The humor is original, the angst palpable, and the heartbreak is utterly crippling. The love I have for these characters is only surpassed by their love for one another.<br><br>The story is told in dual POVs of Tristan and Elizabeth who are both broken by loss. Elizabeth returns home after a few months to find that she has a new neighbor. Tristan Cole is the town’s new asshole. He’s inapproachable, hot as hell, angry, but he eventually sees his own pain reflected back in Elizabeth and her young daughter, Emma the possibilities are endless.<br><br><b>
  <i>”He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.”</i>
</b><br><br>Tristan and Elizabeth bare their losses to one another and slowly start to become a part of one another’s lives. Pretending in the bedroom helps them deal with the pain but does it hinder them from moving on? <br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>Their relationship takes a turn when true feelings for one another develop. The story unfolds with some very clever plot twists and heart stopping action. The supporting characters were a terrific addition and Elizabeth’s best friend, Faye is the SHIT! There is so much humor that evened out the heartbreak and this couple’s fall into love was pretty unforgettable. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br> <br>Overall, this fantastic story is actually up for pre-order for .99 - crazy right? I read the story straight through and I can guarantee if you have loved this author’s previous works this book will exceed your expectations.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><br><i>*ARC provided by the author for an honest review *</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9172019294531054932" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1383009546?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1383009546" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer582859499357132335"><b>*****FIVE+++++++++++++++++ STARS*****</b><br/>(ARC Generously Provided by Author in Exchange For An Honest Review)<br/>{BR with Dee and Mel}<br/><br/><br/><b>BEAUTIFUL!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day."</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d6a77ec873f412c9343ee78f6d14ad9f_zpshpzxtvhf.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443412626i/16358281._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo d6a77ec873f412c9343ee78f6d14ad9f_zpshpzxtvhf.jpg' width='365' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This story was <b>AMAZING</b>!! If I didn't have so many RL distractions I would have devoured this book and honestly I am happy that I had those distractions, because I was able to savor this one!! After having finished this book, I can truly say that Brittainy C Cherry, is one hell of a writer! I would </span>
  <span id="freeText582859499357132335" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE+++++++++++++++++ STARS*****</b><br>(ARC Generously Provided by Author in Exchange For An Honest Review)<br>{BR with Dee and Mel}<br><br><br><b>BEAUTIFUL!!!!!!</b><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/d6a77ec873f412c9343ee78f6d14ad9f_zpshpzxtvhf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443412626i/16358281._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo d6a77ec873f412c9343ee78f6d14ad9f_zpshpzxtvhf.jpg" width="365" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This story was <b>AMAZING</b>!! If I didn't have so many RL distractions I would have devoured this book and honestly I am happy that I had those distractions, because I was able to savor this one!! After having finished this book, I can truly say that Brittainy C Cherry, is one hell of a writer! I would compare her to COHO from her <i>Hopeless</i> and <i>Slammed</i> days. The dialog between the characters goes from laugh out loud hysterical, to tug at your heart strings emotional!!! I literally highlighted the ENTIRE book!!!<br><br><br>Tristan and Lizzie are two people who suffered <b>TREMENDOUS</b> loss. It's the kind of loss that most people never recover from. Each grieve in somewhat different ways but both will feel a strong connection to each other. <br><br><br>Lizzie runs off with her little daughter Emma, and stays with her mom for a while. Being in her own home holds too many memories and she's not ready to face all the ghosts of the past. But living with her mom proves to be much harder for her, so eventually she decides to take her daughter back to their own home. On her first day back in town, she runs into the meanest and most mysterious resident in Meadows Creek. He keeps to himself and can often be seen running barefoot all over town. Lizzie, however, sees past appearances and finds Tristan to be very intriguing. There is something about his stormy eyes that draws her to him.<br><br><br><br>Tristan has become a recluse. A monster. He lives with so much guilt and pain from his past. I tell you, my heart broke wide open for this man. I seriously think if this had happened to me, I would beg God to take my life!! Just thinking now about his pain is making me get all teary eyed. He instantly feels something for Lizzie but fights so hard to push her away because he knows he doesn't deserve her and that eventually he'd only end up hurting her. <br><br><br><br>Eventually Lizzie, along with her little girl, Emma, are able to break through Tristan's walls and they form a very close bond. Lizzie and Tristan eventually take their relationship to the physical level and both even agree that they will use each other while having sex to get over the pain of missing their loved ones. As time passes, they both start to develop true feelings and can no longer go on with their arrangement of pretending they are someone else while being intimate. Now they want to be that special someone to each other, but are holding back for their own reasons, which in my opinion, were misguided.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/32c5116a0ce1b20d597ee03db013d521_zpsy2k2dlnw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443412626i/16358282._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 32c5116a0ce1b20d597ee03db013d521_zpsy2k2dlnw.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>There wasn't much that I didn't love about this story. The secondary characters were well developed and happened to bring some of the laugh out loud moments and then also made some of the emotional scenes, gut wrenching. I loved sweet little Emma and her nickname for Tristan, aka <b>TICK</b>. Oh and those feathers!!!! I never knew the meaning behind "white feathers" but wow, what a beautiful sentiment!! <br><br><br><br>I swooned so hard over Tristan. Any man that would build a library for his woman and write little love post it notes as well, will always win me over hands down!!! <br><br><br><br>There were a couple of things I had issues with. I guess the author added them in to create the angst towards the end, and so I willingly overlooked them because damn I loved this book so HARD! I was sad when I got to the last page. This is the kind of book that makes me so hungry to find that next spectacular read!! <br><br><br>I HIGHLY recommend this one!!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_ms4t02gBWD1rlnzofo1_500_zpsucqtzfc0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441663088ra/16134361.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ms4t02gBWD1rlnzofo1_500_zpsucqtzfc0.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/awesome_zpsnsc9divg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439614525ra/15861359.gif" alt=" photo awesome_zpsnsc9divg.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/giphy_zpsaxtv7ut1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439614525ra/15861358.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsaxtv7ut1.gif" width="365" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/16094605_zps20no7cph.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441329273i/16094660.jpg" alt=" photo 16094605_zps20no7cph.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1351449055" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1351449055" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1351449055?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1351449055" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13977524678928870164"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442778063i/16277319._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ah yes! What can I say? This book was simply wonderful. Damn, the author can write. It reads very fast because it is written so well. Beatiful words make beatiful sentences, which make beautiful story. Loved it all - the angst, the heartbreak, the healing, the falling in love, the humor - all was perfectly balanced. <br/><br/>I don't think I can say much about a plot without spoiling, I think you need to go blind into it, so let's just say th</span>
  <span id="freeText13977524678928870164" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442778063i/16277319._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ah yes! What can I say? This book was simply wonderful. Damn, the author can write. It reads very fast because it is written so well. Beatiful words make beatiful sentences, which make beautiful story. Loved it all - the angst, the heartbreak, the healing, the falling in love, the humor - all was perfectly balanced. <br><br>I don't think I can say much about a plot without spoiling, I think you need to go blind into it, so let's just say that it is about Elizabeth and Tristan, both broken after the tragedies in their pasts, both trying to move on. Their initial meeting doesn't go very well but life throws them together anyway. But will they be enough for each other to heal? Will they be able to put back together their broken hearts? Ahhh, I won't tell, you have to read a book to find out...<br><br>Both main characters were simply amazing. Elizabeth was strong but vulnerable at the same time, she was broken but full of life, I'm happy she was able to see past Tristan's asshole facade and tried to be his friend. Tristan comes as an asshole and dick (oh sorry, I meant Tick), he doesn't want to feel, hates the world and is unapproachable. But once Lizzy and Emma is able to break that emotional wall around his heart, the man is ubelievable - warm, caring, sweet, loving, tender but sexy as hell too. I just wanted to hug him and cuddle and kiss him and take his pain away, seriously people top book boyfriend!<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She undressed me and made love to her past. <br>I slid into her and made love to my ghosts. <br>It wasn’t right, yet somehow it made sense. <br>Her soul was scarred, and mine was burned. <br>But when we were together, the hurting hurt a little less. When we were together, the past wasn’t as painful to take in. When we were together, I never for a second felt alone. ”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>All the emotions were real, I shed a tear, I laughed, I felt the friendship and the love. In addition to exceptionally well written story, you will also get fabulous secondary charcters - little Emma and Zeus the dog, Sam, Faye, they were all so cool. Oh, I also loved Post-it notes they kept writing each other, it was adorable.<br><br>And I just want to give a shout out to Faye, Elizabeth's best friend, who was hilarious. Actually, beside the emotional part, the book had a spot-on dose of humor, it made me laugh out loud more than few times.<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But since we are on the subject, tell me…” Faye said, and I could almost see her grin through the phone. “Did he use tongue? Did he growl? Was he shirtless? Did he motorboat you? Did you touch his abs? Did you lick his sharp jaw? Is he the size of a horse? Did you giddy up? Did you find his Nemo? Did you Grace his Frankie? Did you Justin his Timberlake?”<br><br>"Sometimes when I’m cutting the grass and you’re sitting on your porch reading your dirty books, I see your face blush when you get to a really good part. That Mr. Darcy must have done some crazy shit to Elizabeth’s body. –TC"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> This book is the first part in author's new series, it's a standalone without cliffhanger, written in both POVs. My favorite read of 2015 so far. <u>Highly recommend!!!</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442777872ra/16277304.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b><br><br><u>
  <b>PREREVIEW</b>
</u><br>Drum roll please!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442761246ra/16276026.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I was waiting and waiting and waiting for the best book of the year...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442760725ra/16275929.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And the winner is!!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442760725i/16275930._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Seriously people, pre-order while the price is insanely low, it is worth every penny!<br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Air-He-Breathes-Brittainy-Cherry-ebook/dp/B015L78KRQ/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1442761085&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=the+air+he+breathes" rel="nofollow noopener">The Air He Breathes amazon link</a></span>

<div id="review_1410509992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1410509992" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1410509992?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1410509992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18113920397307169872"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>If you ask me why I started this book,I won't be able to give you an answer.I just...had to.Like I was compelled.Apparently the I-freaking-love-pain part of me was in charge.But if you ask me why I stayed up all night until I finished it and now coffee is the only thing tha</span>
  <span id="freeText18113920397307169872" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>If you ask me why I started this book,I won't be able to give you an answer.I just...had to.Like I was compelled.Apparently the I-freaking-love-pain part of me was in charge.But if you ask me why I stayed up all night until I finished it and now coffee is the only thing that keeps me awake,the answer is simple.<b>My lungs needed air,and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy C. Cherry</a>'s words were my oxygen.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Do I scare you Elizabeth?"<br>"No."<br>"Why?"<br>"Because I see you." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>How do you start over when your whole life is ripped apart?How do you continue breathing when your pain crushes your lungs?How do you live when inside you are dead?When you want to be dead?Elizabeth and Tristan sought the answers to those questions and they found them in each other's haunted eyes and scarred soul.At first they used their bodies to feel whole again,to feel wanted and loved when in fact they didn't think they deserved it.They had to learn how to cope with their losses and their guilt,to remember the past while they faced the present and planned the future.They had to learn how to love again.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The magic is in the tiny moments. The small touches, the gentle smiles, the quiet laughs. The magic is about living for today and allowing yourself to breathe and be happy. My dear boy, to love is the magic.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>What started as an <b>unhealthy and twisted relationship</b> turned into a <b>tender,beautiful love story</b>.While reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564446.The_Air_He_Breathes__Elements___1_" title="The Air He Breathes (Elements, #1) by Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">The Air He Breathes</a> I experienced so many emotions at once,<b>as if a storm was brewing in my chest,as if my chest would explode into a rain of colours,green for anger,black for grief,red for pain,yellow for joy,white for love</b>.With those colours <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy C. Cherry</a> painted the canvas of my soul and she signed it with blood taken from my own heart.The heart that ached for the trials Tristan and Elizabeth went through,that bled when they lost the battles against their demons,that warmed up when they started falling in love,that shattered when they were torn apart.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“As long as air moves in and out of my lungs … as long as I breathe, I will fight for you. I will fight for us.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When a book makes you try to hold back your <b>tears</b> and a few pages later makes you burst into <b>maniacal laughter</b>,it is a good book.There were so many quotes that were touching,so many lines I highlighted because they inspired me,so many scenes that were beautifully written.It wasn't flawless,I didn't like the time gaps that took you weeks or months later because sometimes they were abrupt and I wanted more details about what happened in between,but that didn't prevent me from loving <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7121791.Brittainy_C__Cherry" title="Brittainy C. Cherry" rel="nofollow noopener">Brittainy C. Cherry</a>'s writing.Her characters were so <b>painfully realistic</b>,Tristan and Elizabeth healed each other and filled the void their losses had created step by step,each step a small victory against the monster of grief and death.They made mistakes,they fucked up what they'd created,but Elizabeth saw the human beneath Tristan's jerkish attitude,and Tristan saw his redemption in Elizabeth's smile.I loved the relationship between Tristan and Emma,Elizabeth's daughter,they were so silly and adorable.I loved Faye and her inappropriate comments.I loved the brutal plot twist towards the end.And I loved that I could not sleep because every time I closed my eyes I saw white feathers.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449938670ra/17360238.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><u>
  <b>Five bruised and bleeding stars for two bruised and bleeding hearts.</b>
</u><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It was obvious what she was to me,it was so clear why I always wanted her near.<br>She was simply the air I breathed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="18113920397307169872" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=slow-burn-baby">slow-burn-baby</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=love-hate">love-hate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=heartbreaking-i-cried-a-river">heartbreaking-i-cried-a-river</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396488414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12458119196834363201">★★★★★ <b>4.5 Stars</b> ★★★★★ <br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/><a href='http://amzn.to/1LasfXh' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> | <a href='http://amzn.to/1Oy3jtc' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a></b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443012862i/16306598._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Wow! I could read this story it all over again, I had the serious case of feels - this book was an amazing read! It was a fabulous combination of interesting characters, humour, sadness and hope. On top of that we are gifted with an aloof hero as the main character that you just want to cuddle and do dirty things with in equal measure.<br/><br/>The Air He Breathes is about two broken people who have both suffered a huge loss in their lives and are tryi</span>
  <span id="freeText12458119196834363201" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>4.5 Stars</b> ★★★★★ <br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br><a href="http://amzn.to/1LasfXh" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> | <a href="http://amzn.to/1Oy3jtc" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a></b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443012862i/16306598._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Wow! I could read this story it all over again, I had the serious case of feels - this book was an amazing read! It was a fabulous combination of interesting characters, humour, sadness and hope. On top of that we are gifted with an aloof hero as the main character that you just want to cuddle and do dirty things with in equal measure.<br><br>The Air He Breathes is about two broken people who have both suffered a huge loss in their lives and are trying to get through day by day. After having spent the past year mourning her husband, Elizabeth returns home from an extended visit at her mothers, back to the house that she shared with her husband. She is still incredibly raw from her loss, but is trying to be a whole person again for her five year old daughter, Emma.<br><br>Back in a familiar place, she is feeling like she will never be the woman she was before, and even surrounded by her friends and family she has no-one to turn to who understands her pain. That is until she meets her next door neighbour, Tristan.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443012862i/16306599._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tristan has completely shut down from anyone, since he lost his wife and son and is a shell of a man merely surviving each day through pain, with only his dog Zeus and his boss, the eccentric Mr. Henson for company, he is extremely lonely.<br><br>When Elizabeth and Tristan meet, the connection is instant, but the friendship isn't and so their relationship goes through many different stages, from indifference to lust to friendship to love.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"You're beautiful. You're a beautiful, broken kind of monster."</b>
</blockquote> <br>What starts off as them using each other to remember their past loved ones, turns into something very beautiful and I for one though that it was a very unique and engaging story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I wasn't him. She wasn't her. But my God, it felt good to lie to ourselves."</b>
</blockquote> <br>Not only did I fall in love with the main characters pretty much off the bat, but the relationship between Tristan &amp; Emma pretty much sealed the deal. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443020983i/16307429._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To top it off, we had Elizabeth's best friend Faye, who was a hoot and balanced out all the sad that was within the pages. So many great quotes from the supporting cast, including this one which has become my new favourite mantra.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Sometimes life is weird. You just have to deal with the weirdness and hope that you find some weirdos who will move forward with you."</b>
</blockquote> <br>There was a bit of drama towards the end which felt came a little out of left field, hence my half star reduction, but really it was a minor blip on my radar and would consider this a five star read in every other way.<br><br>I would highly recommend this book to anyone who enjoys a gut-wrenching read that will make you cry and then lift you up in the best way. A fantastic job from Brittainy C. Cherry!<br><br><b>This is a standalone contemporary romance, told in dual POV.</b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i> <br> <br><div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1284236116" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12629255807971696184"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> The Air He Breathes <br/><b>Series:</b> Romance Elements #1, can be read as a standalone<br/><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br/><b>Release Date: </b> September 25, 2015<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 - 5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. no<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442670112i/16267049.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The Air He Breathes is perfectly written story. A story that took me on amazing journey full of feelings and emotions so real I can still feel my heart crumbling. This is one of those novels that stay with readers forever – the print it leaves on soul too strong to ever fade aw</span>
  <span id="freeText12629255807971696184" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> The Air He Breathes <br><b>Series:</b> Romance Elements #1, can be read as a standalone<br><b>Author:</b> Brittainy C. Cherry<br><b>Release Date: </b> September 25, 2015<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 - 5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. no<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442670112i/16267049.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Air He Breathes is perfectly written story. A story that took me on amazing journey full of feelings and emotions so real I can still feel my heart crumbling. This is one of those novels that stay with readers forever – the print it leaves on soul too strong to ever fade away. And even if the details of it will blur with time, the depth and the meaning of the story will definitely still be remembered. <br><br>That’s why Brittainy C. Cherry is one of my favorite authors – the way she can tug on my heartstrings is unmistakably beautiful and moving. She simply creates a plot and characters so broken yet real that the reading experience is so powerful you feel overwhelmed with. In the best way of course.<br><br><blockquote>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</blockquote><br><br><b>"The magic is in the tiny moments. The small touches, the gentle smiles, the quiet laughs. The magic is about living for today and allowing yourself to breathe and be happy. My dear boy, to love is the magic."</b><br><blockquote>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442940238i/16296351.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Air He Breathes tells a story about two people who had just survived the loss of the loved ones. They are both broken and having a hard time dealing with the death of their soulmate.<br><br>When Elizabeth lost her husband the only thing that had the strength to pull her just a little bit of the darkness was her little daughter Emma. If not her Liz would probably have lost herself in despair. <br><br>Tristan had even less luck. His eight year old son was killed in an accident right along with his wife. Having no one to focus on Tristan completely crumbled. He became a recluse, believing he doesn’t deserve to have people love him…<br><br>Due to serendipity Tristan moved into house next door to Elizabeth. Together they learn how to let go, how to heal and feel free again – but it’s not pretty. <br><br><blockquote>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</blockquote><br><br><b>"Her soul was scarred, and mine was burned. <br>But when we were together, the hurting hurt a little less. When we were together, the past wasn’t as painful to take in. When we were together, I never for a second felt alone.."</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442940238i/16296352.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>On the pages of The Air He Breathes you can find everything what makes a story perfect - from the heartbreak to the silly dose of humor, from sensual and intense romance and intimacy to very well pictured secondary characters and friendship. <br><br>This book exceed my expectations - it was angstier and sexier that I thought was possible. It had as well the most moving and touching plotline - it simply left me breathless. It teaches that there is beauty in every tragedy and that love comes with loss yet still a single moment of happiness is worth the pain.<br><br>Reasuming, Brittainy C. Cherry yet again nailed it! I think she only gets better and better at creating realistic, beautiful and unique plotlines. I cannot wait to read her next book, because even right now I’m pretty sure it would be the bomb. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442940239i/16296353.jpg" width="400" height='300"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</blockquote><br>	<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427385833i/14267472._SX540_.jpg" width="400” height=" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter"
