<div id="review_1398059526" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1398059526" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1398059526?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1398059526" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12021335710483578142"><a href='http://amzn.to/1ixwy1M' rel='nofollow noopener'>LIVE!</a><br/><br/>I have to say my biggest fear is losing my husband. He isn’t perfect, but he is my soulmate and I can’t imagine a life without him in it. Thank God I haven’t experienced this type of loss, because reading about it nearly broken my heart in two. Not every author or story can make me feel the pain the characters are feeling, but Brittainy’s writing makes me feel <b>everything</b>. I felt their loss, their grief, and their doubts. I felt their love, their healing and their hope. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Sometimes th</blockquote></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12021335710483578142" style="display:none"><a href="http://amzn.to/1ixwy1M" rel="nofollow noopener">LIVE!</a><br><br>I have to say my biggest fear is losing my husband. He isn’t perfect, but he is my soulmate and I can’t imagine a life without him in it. Thank God I haven’t experienced this type of loss, because reading about it nearly broken my heart in two. Not every author or story can make me feel the pain the characters are feeling, but Brittainy’s writing makes me feel <b>everything</b>. I felt their loss, their grief, and their doubts. I felt their love, their healing and their hope. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your loved one was remembering how to breathe.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Elizabeth Bailey is a single mother to Emma. When we first meet Liz it has been a year since her husband’s death and she is moving back to their home in Meadow’s Creek. Meadow Creek is a small community and she is immediately bombarded with nosey neighbors and caring friends and family. Despite being surrounded by family and friends she still feels this deep loneliness, an ache in her heart that won’t let up. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443051583i/16310536._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tristan Cole isn’t from Meadow’s Creek, it’s just the town he ran to when everything he loved was taken from him. His world was shattered when he lost his wife and son. His grief has turned to anger and he doesn’t hold back. At first glance it’s easy to believe he is just a grumpy, self-centered, rude asshole, that is certainly Liz’s first impression. She isn’t thrilled to learn Tristan is her neighbor now, nor is he pleased to see Liz and Emma next door. Tristan is burdened down by his grief. He has let his pain fester, has isolated anyone who cares about him, and is completely alone. <br><br>There is this insane beautifulness to Tristan and Liz’s connection. They are both lost, lonely and searching. They are both grief stricken, stuck and terrified to move on, afraid to forget. They are stagnate in their lives and consumed by their hopelessness, until they finally accept help from each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443051583i/16310537._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Tristan and Liz’s relationship was perfect. They are not your typical hero and heroine, they are two damaged souls in desperate need of healing. Together they help each other grieve and eventually move forward. I absolutely loved these two together. I loved how Tristan is damaged and afraid. I could feel Tristan’s pain and loss, and my heart broken for him. I loved how Liz was the light he needed, even in her own grief she offered a solace to Tristan.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"One must know what it feels like to be weak in order to really find their own strength.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><i>The Air He Breathes</i> was perfection on paper. It was devastating sad, but had these moments I found hope in. It was heavy and emotional, but had these amazing light, fun, humorous moments. Brittainy built this deep soulful connection between Tristan and Liz, and I loved it. But she also added in these perfect, fun, even crude moments that made me laugh out loud. I also love how she was able to captivate and surprise me. She delivered on all fronts!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443051583i/16310538._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When you are looking for a book that is hopeful, beautiful, uplifting, unique, emotional and sexy this is the book you need to read. I will never forget this story or how I felt when reading it. Definitely one of my Top 2015 Reads!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br>
  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-is-Sexy-Book-Blog/717861984979600" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574956.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13095060-beverly" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/readingissexybo/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1386461175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13567262482933884695"><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443454529i/16362495._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are tons of wonderful reviews for this story, so I will keep it short and sweet.<br/><br/><i>The Air He Breathes</i> is an emotional story, about two people who have suffered enormous loss, but together they find a way to live and love again. <br/><br/>I enjoyed this read, but the drama and coincidences during the last 10-20% was a bit much, in my opinion. That said, I still found this to be a great story, overall.</span>
  <span id="freeText13567262482933884695" style="display:none"><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443454529i/16362495._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are tons of wonderful reviews for this story, so I will keep it short and sweet.<br><br><i>The Air He Breathes</i> is an emotional story, about two people who have suffered enormous loss, but together they find a way to live and love again. <br><br>I enjoyed this read, but the drama and coincidences during the last 10-20% was a bit much, in my opinion. That said, I still found this to be a great story, overall.</span>

  <span id="freeText9609641718239814791" style="display:none"><b>My God, this book was so beautiful. &lt;3<br> I cried too much while I was reading it... :(</b> <br><br><i>"Right before I turned to leave, a small white feather came floating down from above and landed against my arm. A wave of comfort washed over me as I nodded. “I’ll be okay. I’ll be good,” I muttered, knowing that it was a kiss from my loved ones. Show me where it hurts the most. I want to see your soul.” <br><br>“Even though I was death, she took the time to resuscitate me. She breathed life back into my soul. She brought me back from the shadows.” <br><br>“Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your loved ones was remembering how to breathe.” <br><br>“You know that place between nightmares and dreams? The place where tomorrows never come and yesterdays don't hurt anymore? The place where your heart beats in sync with mine? The place where time doesn't exist, and it's easy to breathe? <br>I want to live there with you.” <br><br>“It’s easier with you.” <br>“What’s easier with me?” <br>His hand found my lower back. My hips arched toward him, our bodies slowly becoming one. He ran his fingers against my neck as I closed my eyes, and he spoke softly into my soul. “Being alive.” <br><br>“He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.” <br><br>“As long as air moves in and out of my lungs … as long as I breathe, I will fight for you. I will fight for us.” <br><br>"Right before I turned to leave, a small white feather came floating down from above and landed against my arm. A wave of comfort washed over me as I nodded. “I’ll be okay. I’ll be good,” I muttered, knowing that it was a kiss from my loved ones. I knew I would be okay one day, because it was obvious that I wasn’t alone."<br><br>“Because at the end of the day, it’s not about the tarot cards, or the crystals, or the special teas. That’s not where the magic lives. The magic is in the tiny moments. The small touches, the gentle smiles, the quiet laughs. The magic is about living for today and allowing yourself to breathe and be happy. My dear boy, to love is the magic.” <br><br>“She undressed me and made love to her past. I slid into her and made love to my ghosts. It wasn’t right, yet somehow it made sense. Her soul was scarred, and mine was burned. But when we were together, the hurting hurt a little less. When we were together, the past wasn’t as painful to take in. When we were together, I never for a second felt alone.”</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5194415922669797860">4.5 Stars<br/><br/><br/>I'm in love. The Air He Breathes is my first book by Brittainy C. Cherry, but it won't be my last. Damn but she tore my heart out, and slowly pieced it back together with this emotional read. I loved both the hero and the heroine. I knew going into the read that the main couple lost their husband/wife and that they start out using each other. I really thought it would have bothered me more. It was why I have held off reading it for so long. But it was written so well that it didn't both</span>
  <span id="freeText5194415922669797860" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br /><br />I'm in love. The Air He Breathes is my first book by Brittainy C. Cherry, but it won't be my last. Damn but she tore my heart out, and slowly pieced it back together with this emotional read. I loved both the hero and the heroine. I knew going into the read that the main couple lost their husband/wife and that they start out using each other. I really thought it would have bothered me more. It was why I have held off reading it for so long. But it was written so well that it didn't bother me at all. I love that they stopped pretending pretty fast. I also love that even though they started out using each other I didn't feel either one was second to the dead ex. This book was just wow no words. I really loved it. The only reason it's not a full 5 stars is I was a tad bit upset that Tristan left for so long. But still I could kinda of understand it too. Other than that it was amazing. I can't believe I waited so long to pick this book up!</span>

<div id="review_1352773300" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1352773300" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1352773300?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1352773300" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12719563101126396638"><b>4.5 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443793534i/16411883.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>“The Air He Breathes”</i> is one of the most touching romance story I’ve read this year. It was simply perfect, beautifully, beautifully written and so touching. It was heartbreaking, emotional and also heartwarming, a story that definitely will stay with me for a while. It’s a story about loss, forgiveness and learning to love and live again. It was exactly what I expected from one of my favorite authors who every time with her amazing words manages to create an outstanding story. <br/><br/>Now t</span>
  <span id="freeText12719563101126396638" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443793534i/16411883.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>“The Air He Breathes”</i> is one of the most touching romance story I’ve read this year. It was simply perfect, beautifully, beautifully written and so touching. It was heartbreaking, emotional and also heartwarming, a story that definitely will stay with me for a while. It’s a story about loss, forgiveness and learning to love and live again. It was exactly what I expected from one of my favorite authors who every time with her amazing words manages to create an outstanding story. <br><br>Now take a moment and imagine you lost your husband/wife, the father/mother of your child, the man/woman who represented everything for you, your reason to live and breathe, your world. Honestly I can’t imagine losing my husband. I will be more than broken, more than devastated, more than lost. The main characters in this book, Elizabeth and Tristan have experienced a huge loss losing their loved ones, their world, a husband and wife and son respectively. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The hardest part about losing someone you love is the fact that you also lose yourself.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Elizabeth lost herself when she lost her husband in a car accident. Everyday it’s a struggle. She is trying her best to move on, to live, to breathe, to be a mother for her little daughter. She doesn’t think she knows how to do all that anymore, but she knows she has to stay strong. She knows if it hadn’t been for her daughter she would have lost herself to the grief. After the tragic accident Lizzie and her daughter, Emma went to stay with her mother, but now a year later they are ready to go home. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“People in town called him an asshole, and I could see why. He wasn’t nice, he wasn’t stable, and he was broken in all of the wrong and right places, but I couldn’t blame him for his coldness.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>When Lizzie meets Tristan, the new man in town, the town jerk, the man everyone avoids, she’s drawn to him. His sad eyes tell a tragic story. He’s like her, broken. She can tell. Tristan lost his reason to live a while ago and now he’s changed man, a broken man who doesn’t want to live anymore or to have a family and friends. Lizzie wants to be his friend, she wants to talk to each other, to heal each other, but Tristan doesn’t want to do anything with her or with her daughter. He’s angry and bitter at first, but eventually both Lizzie and Emma manage to warm his heart. Lizzie makes him hope and feel. They are attracted to each other, but both of them are hesitant to get involved in something new and possible dangerous for their hearts. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He and I together was a terrible idea. We were both unstable, we were both shattered, and there was no getting around it. He was thunder, I was lightning, and we were seconds away from creating the perfect storm.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>They start using each other to remember their past loved ones, but eventually what they initially started becomes so much more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She undressed me and made love to her past.<br> 	I slid into her and made love to my ghosts.<br> 	It wasn’t right, yet somehow it made sense.<br> 	Her soul was scarred, and mine was burned.<br>But when we were together, the hurting hurt a little less. When we were together, the past wasn’t as painful to take in. When we were together, I never for a second felt alone.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was one beautiful story that I guarantee will move you to tears. Like I mentioned, this author’s words are simply perfect and evoked so many different emotions in me. Both Lizzie and Tristan are remarkable, well developed characters, characters I fell in love with so hard from the start. Lizzie was broken, but she was such a great strong heroine. I loved her relationship with her daughter Emma and the way she loved her. She was such a great mother to her. She also was a great friend to Faye, her best friend and later to Tristan. Tristan was portrayed as a jerk at first, but I never hated him or judged him, because let’s face it, loss can changed everyone of us. His story broke my heart and some scenes from his past were really gut-wrenching. I wanted so much to see him smile and hope again, fall in love and learn to breathe again. And fortunately he will learn how to.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Do you ever think of me in a way that is more than a friendship?” When she looked into my eyes, she had to see the answer. I felt her soul staring deep into mine. Her eyes were full of wondering interest and her beauty was softened by an air of mystery.<br> 	I blinked once. “Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Lizzie and Tristan’s relationship was fantastically done. I loved the slow build relationship and how gradually they became more than friends. Their connections was palpable from the beginning and later you can actually feel how much they feel for each other, how much they mean for each other. <br><br>As for the supportive characters, what can I say? They were simply fantastic. I loved Faye, Lizzie’s best friend. She was a great person. She was kind, funny and at times everything Lizzie need it. Emma, Lizzie’s daughter was simply adorable and like I said I loved the relationship between these two. It warmed my heart. But what I really loved was the relationship between Emma and Tristan. Their interaction were amazing, so damn sweet and put big smile on my face. <br><br>Overall, a wonderful emotional read that I highly recommend it!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Sometimes life is weird. You just have to deal with the weirdness and hope that you find some weirdos who will move forward with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="12719563101126396638" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1451208440?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer16696222603077136882">My first 5 star read for 2016. <br/><br/><b>"In the blink of an eye, in one moment's time, everything I knew about life changed."</b><br/><br/>I loved this opening quote because it's holds true for all of us. It's relatable and makes us feel the story even deeper. Life is unpredictable and our paths can be altered in just the blink of an eye. Adventuring with the characters on their journey from hurt-to-healing-to-finding love is one that kept me up reading late into the night. <br/><br/>I enjoyed <b>The Air He Breathes</b> even though I </span>
  <span id="freeText16696222603077136882" style="display:none">My first 5 star read for 2016. <br><br><b>"In the blink of an eye, in one moment's time, everything I knew about life changed."</b><br><br>I loved this opening quote because it's holds true for all of us. It's relatable and makes us feel the story even deeper. Life is unpredictable and our paths can be altered in just the blink of an eye. Adventuring with the characters on their journey from hurt-to-healing-to-finding love is one that kept me up reading late into the night. <br><br>I enjoyed <b>The Air He Breathes</b> even though I had a moment where this book dipped below 5 stars for me. I found the ending with Tanner to be over the top drama that didn't match up with the flow of the story. After pondering my star rating I decided that for 95% of the book it was definitely worthy of five stars and that OTT moment is something I can look past. Alright enough about that part because the rest of the book was fantastic. <br><br>For those who haven't read it yet...what are you waiting for?! <br><br><b>STANDALONE</b><br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1384081925" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1384081925?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=broken-heroine">broken-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=epic-all-time-read">epic-all-time-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=top-shelf-quality">top-shelf-quality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=widow-widower">widow-widower</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=douchebag">douchebag</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=sep2015">sep2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1384081925" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4759745072285865204"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png' width='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Title:</b> The Air He Breathes<br/><b>Series:</b> Elements #1<br/><b>Author:</b> Brittany C. Cherry<br/><b>Release date: </b> September 25, 2015<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b>HEA</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443189054i/16331287._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430579277ra/14730165.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>In a blink of an eye, in one moment's time, everything I knew about life changed.</b><br/><br/>This is my first Brittany C. Cherry book, (stupid, stupid me) and this is one thing I can tell you with complete confidence: when you pick up a book from this author, you're holding something precious in your hands. I had no idea what I was missing out on all thi</span>
  <span id="freeText4759745072285865204" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396539003i/9148958.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430781898i/14762044.png" width="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Title:</b> The Air He Breathes<br><b>Series:</b> Elements #1<br><b>Author:</b> Brittany C. Cherry<br><b>Release date: </b> September 25, 2015<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b>HEA</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443189054i/16331287._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430579277ra/14730165.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>In a blink of an eye, in one moment's time, everything I knew about life changed.</b><br><br>This is my first Brittany C. Cherry book, (stupid, stupid me) and this is one thing I can tell you with complete confidence: when you pick up a book from this author, you're holding something precious in your hands. I had no idea what I was missing out on all this time and I feel like I'm finally realizing how deprived I've been. Believe me, this author has hit my auto-buy list-solidly. Sometimes an author has a voice that really speaks to you. Immediately, completely, and perfectly. That's what I feel here. If I could give this book a million more stars I would. Within the first chapter I was already laughing, crying, and sometimes both at the same time. Can you say that about many books? This book is something special, you need to introduce yourself to this hauntingly beautiful story.<br><br>It's a story of overwhelming, soul crushing grief. A story of pain. The kind that shreds you and dehumanizes you into someone you don't recognize. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443191367i/16331517._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's about finding strength through that brokenness and pulling yourself out of the darkness even when you don't think you can. And these emotions were expressed with such crystal clarity, I felt every bit of hurt these characters were going through. The loss of loved ones is a subject that I can imagine isn't easy to write about. But it was done with sensitivity and it just...moved me. There's no other way to say it. <br><br>Both Tristan and Elizabeth have lost a loved one. Her husband, his wife and young son. They're going through the motions of life, but the've been dead inside since the day of their loss. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443191449i/16331527._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hurt so bad for them seeing their emptiness and loneliness. Especially for Tristan who didn't even have the comfort of his child to cushion the blow. Elizabeth pushes on-for her daughter. But Tristan lives only with the memories of what was taken from him. And his wounds have cut him so deeply that he lashes out at anyone who crosses his path. Even though he was hateful and hurtful to Elizabeth, their common link bound them together and wouldn't let her write him off. Looking in his eyes was like looking into a mirror and she only wanted to get closer. <br><br><b>He was hard to look at, because he was so broken, but every scarred part of his existence seemed to draw me in.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443193762ra/16331755.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The relationship she had with her best friend was the perfect way to deal with the difficult emotions you go through in this book. They were hilarious together-every scene between them had me smiling and chuckling at Faye's outrageousness. Elizabeth's sense of humor added a lightness to the story that balanced out all the dark. Without it, I don't know if I could have handled the harshness so easily. <br><br><b><i>Hmm.</i> It seemed he wasn't a morning, afternoon, or night kind of person, so he had that going for him.</b><br><br>The beginning of their relationship grows from a very unhealthy place. They're both still just trying to survive. But after their dislike wears off, they evolve into something more. But it's not real. They cling to each other, but they're only clinging to ghosts. They're fine with that, in fact they need it desperately. To feel like they're holding on to a piece of their past through each other. This is completely wrong and it was like taking 10 steps back in their healing process. But in some small way, maybe it was needed for them to break out their torment and inability to move on. Pushing past this crutch, they were finally able to give each other what they really needed. Someone to listen. Someone to see them. They come from a parallel place and no one else could understand the emotions they battle every day except each other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443194458ra/16331797.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Everyone in this town is afraid of me. Do I scare you, Elizabeth?" he whispered, his breaths against my lips.<br>"No."<br>"Why not?"<br>"Because I see you."</b><br><br>We see Tristan's hard heart start to soften being around Elizabeth and her daughter Emma. The way he symbolically gave her messages from her father with the feathers was enough to make me cry like a baby. I can't even tell you how many times I was overwhelmed with emotion. My whole brain was screaming and my throat was clogged for pretty much the majority of the book. If I could have soaked in every word slowly and made this experience stretch out longer I would have. I just don't have the words to explain how incredible this book was. It was pure, raw, unfiltered emotion, I loved every minute of it. We see the bottomless lows they go through and that's what makes them soar so high in the end. <i>Read. This. Book.</i> You won't ever forget it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443193103i/16331703._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>**When I finished this book, this song came to mind. It's like it was made to explain how this book makes you feel. Beautiful, haunting, and lovely. Listen to it along with the book. It made me cry.<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-gB4iD6H7XI&amp;list=PL-8iiR7S-tryFbN4JGjiWRTbd1SSwj25e&amp;index=9">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-gB4i...</a><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON:   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1395659685" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1395659685?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=swoon-worthy-guys">swoon-worthy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=top-2015-reads">top-2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=all-time-fav-author">all-time-fav-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=killing-me-with-sexual-tension">killing-me-with-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1395659685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16271040817606603483"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442758290i/16275687.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"But as long as air moves in and out of my lungs, as long as I breathe, I will fight for you. I will fight for us."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Once again, Brittainy C Cherry has delivered a top-notch romance read and dare I say rather effortlessly. Her previous work, <u>Art & Soul</u> easily snagged one of my top reads of 2015 and so does this one. Right from the prologue, I already knew this book would put me through for an emotional ride.<br/><br/>This is a story about loss, forgiveness, redemption and finding love agai</span>
  <span id="freeText16271040817606603483" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442758290i/16275687.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"But as long as air moves in and out of my lungs, as long as I breathe, I will fight for you. I will fight for us."</i>
</b><br><br>Once again, Brittainy C Cherry has delivered a top-notch romance read and dare I say rather effortlessly. Her previous work, <u>Art &amp; Soul</u> easily snagged one of my top reads of 2015 and so does this one. Right from the prologue, I already knew this book would put me through for an emotional ride.<br><br>This is a story about loss, forgiveness, redemption and finding love again. Both MCs, <b>Tristan</b> and <b>Elizabeth</b> have experienced a crippling loss by losing their most loved ones and stumbled upon each other when they became neighbours. Tristan is the least of welcoming and puts up an icy exterior to every person he comes in contact with. Even after an attempt by Elizabeth who saved his dog, Tristan wants nothing to do with this woman. <br><br>Eventually when they realised they shared a common loss, they saw a chance to make their pain more bearable by holding onto their past through each other. Two broken souls who desperately seeks the feelings they once felt and longed for. But will they be able to move forward if they keep latching onto their pasts? <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"She undressed me and made love to her past. I slid into her and made love to my ghosts."</i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435r/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've said it before but I'll say it again: this author has a way of writing so beautifully that will tug at your heartstrings in every book she puts out. From the admirable characters whether main or supporting, you can't help but be smitten by all of them. Even right down to the golden retriever, Zeus. She brings the light moments into the read by bringing in characters like Faye who says the darnest things that cracked me up like mad! But most of all, this author writes like she pours her heart and soul into every read because you will <i>truly</i> feel for these characters and experience their love, their loss and their heartbreak of it all. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"The magic is in the tiny moments. The small touches, the gentle smiles, the quiet laughs. The magic is about living for today and allowing yourself to breathe and be happy. My dear boy, to love is the magic."</i>
</blockquote><br> Easily another of my top read of 2015, <u>The Air He Breathes</u> promises a love story that teaches you that with loss, there can still be love. There is beauty in tragedy and there can always be more than one happily ever afters in your life. This story will gripped you from start till end and also promises some unexpected twists that will shock you. <b>I'd highly recommend this read for sure!!</b> <br><br>P/S: It's only $0.99 for this crazily amazing book!! Pre-order now -&gt; <a href="http://amzn.to/1Qq6pgc" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435r/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b><br><br><i><u>The Air He Breathes</u> is a contemporary romance standalone read. This is also the first standalone book in her Romance Elements series.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer13266964803210698118">The cheese factor was high with this one.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445438185i/16650595.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I thought I'd sink into this and roll around like a two year old in a ball pit but instead I just sank.   <span id="freeText13266964803210698118" style="display:none">The cheese factor was high with this one.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445438185i/16650595.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I thought I'd sink into this and roll around like a two year old in a ball pit but instead I just sank. It started off okay, with the buildup to the meet-cute and Tristan's ass-holery front and center. As soon as we established how "broken" the protagonists were, though, it all went downhill. There were so many quotes that made me cringe, but the first one that made me question whether or not I'd finish was this tidbit. People just don't <b>say</b> shit like this. It's like cheesy role play.<br><br><b>"We'll use each other to remember them?"<br><br>"Only if you want to." <br><br>"This sounds like a terrible idea, in the best kind of way."<br><br>"There's still this giant part of me that misses Jamie every day. I skimmed some of the rest, but gave up a little over the halfway point. </span>

<div id="review_1446455948" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1446455948" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1446455948?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26721257-the-air-he-breathes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2015">favourites-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1446455948" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8190894762436661579"><strong>It was worth taking that next breath.</strong><br/><br/>Life's a funny thing. What's worse, finding out your loved one has two months to live or will die instantly in a car crash? Both are bad, but when you lose the opportunity for one last goodbye, how do you move on? The Air He Breathes was one of the best and emotional reads I've experienced in a long time. I cried through the whole thing and continually questioned how on earth I could come out the other side with a smile on my face. For two people to have that</span>
  <span id="freeText8190894762436661579" style="display:none"><strong>It was worth taking that next breath.</strong><br><br>Life's a funny thing. What's worse, finding out your loved one has two months to live or will die instantly in a car crash? Both are bad, but when you lose the opportunity for one last goodbye, how do you move on? The Air He Breathes was one of the best and emotional reads I've experienced in a long time. I cried through the whole thing and continually questioned how on earth I could come out the other side with a smile on my face. For two people to have that much pain in their lives and still manage to keep breathing was inspiring. I will try and remember (for the next 24 hours at least) to make the most of each day and tell my loved ones how much they mean to me.<br><br>The writing style flowed well and even though there were a few flashbacks, which I'm not normally a fan of, they helped you get a better understanding of how things had played out previously. The characters were brilliantly crafted with the supporting ones bringing the story to life. There were intimate scenes to show the strong connection between Tristan and Elizabeth, but they weren't over the top or put in to make the story better. They were just there to show the couple's progression. The relationship with Tristan and Emma was beautifully told and you could see that the author wasn't using Elizabeth's daughter as a replacement for him.<br><br>I'm not the sort of person who enjoys stories that makes you weep, but this one was special and will stay with me for a long while to come. Ms Cherry has made me stop and think before judging people by their looks or even their actions....maybe there's a reason for the monster to keep breathing. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1548709401i/26982519.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="8190894762436661579" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1397431050" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1397431050" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1397431050?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1397431050" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8744867169201728160"><b>4 "Big, fat, giant TICK!" Stars!<br/><br/><blockquote><i>Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your love ones was remembering how to breathe.</i></blockquote>
<br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/AD9CE88E-E6C8-40A4-BDA3-A2EC6DAF3CAB_zpsovpkrcju.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443571771i/16378092._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo AD9CE88E-E6C8-40A4-BDA3-A2EC6DAF3CAB_zpsovpkrcju.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/><br/>The Air He Breathes</b> is a first <b> Brittainy C Cherry</b> book for me. I'll admit the book buzz was contagious and I pretty much dropped everything to read this. Problem with buzz books for me is they tend to give me a false high expectation. Because of that, I forced myself to read very few reviews...but I don't live under a rock. This book was everywhere on social media- well </span>
  <span id="freeText8744867169201728160" style="display:none"><b>4 "Big, fat, giant TICK!" Stars!<br><br><blockquote><i>Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your love ones was remembering how to breathe.</i></blockquote>
<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/AD9CE88E-E6C8-40A4-BDA3-A2EC6DAF3CAB_zpsovpkrcju.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443571771i/16378092._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo AD9CE88E-E6C8-40A4-BDA3-A2EC6DAF3CAB_zpsovpkrcju.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><br>The Air He Breathes</b> is a first <b> Brittainy C Cherry</b> book for me. I'll admit the book buzz was contagious and I pretty much dropped everything to read this. Problem with buzz books for me is they tend to give me a false high expectation. Because of that, I forced myself to read very few reviews...but I don't live under a rock. This book was everywhere on social media- well deserved, I might add. With that being said...<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I love the premise of a book with two protagonists suffering a major loss. Nothing produces insta-angst like that. But Ms Cherry captured my heart with a little five-year old spit-fire more than anything else.<b> Elizabeth </b>is a single mother, a widow, trying to get through her grief one step at a time. When taking off to live with her mother gets stale, she decides to move back to her home, a small town filled with gossip mongers and a house filled with memories...and a lawn grown up to her knees. What she didn't bank on is hitting a man's Golden Retriever just as she entered town. A man that was clearly jogging...barefoot. And he's not too happy. How is this her fault?<br><br><br><br>From the very beginning, we were gifted with a fantastic banter between a clearly <s>assholish</s> disgruntled hero and a sweet heroine that still has a backbone to defend herself. He too is suffering from the loss of both his wife and child and chooses to be a grade-A <i>dick</i> because, quite frankly he doesn't deserve anyone's sympathy or compassion. At least that's what he tells himself. Keep the walls up and the sympathizers at bay so he can wallow alone. So he chooses to withdraw from townsfolk by being the town asshole. Something about <b>Tristan Cole </b>drew <b>Elizabeth</b> to him. Yes, his bark was pretty ferocious but she didn't sway from getting under his tough exterior. Couple that with her adorable daughter <b>Emma,</b> and <b>Tristan </b>doesn't stand a chance.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Nothing I love more in a love story than that angsty tug of war from within. Of two people fighting their attractions for whatever reasons. So when the two MCs decide to take their release within each other, it was fantastic and steaming!<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/F7556C5C-854A-4DA7-BCD4-308E15B403ED_zpswwuamhka.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443571771i/16378093._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo F7556C5C-854A-4DA7-BCD4-308E15B403ED_zpswwuamhka.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>I could seriously highlight 90% of this book. It's simply very beautiful and I actually took quite a bit away from some of the philosophical quotes within this novel. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/review%20art/BB04FDBE-0090-4B1E-89E6-CAA7B0055E7D_zpsnxxohl0y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443571771i/16378094._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BB04FDBE-0090-4B1E-89E6-CAA7B0055E7D_zpsnxxohl0y.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>Yes, sometimes I found myself thinking, "What guy really talks like this?" The sap factor was high but my heart swooned nonetheless. Sometimes we like alpha tough brooding heroes, but Tristan is more the damaged "bark is worse than his bite" sympathetic-type character. Secondary characters almost stole the show for me. Her daughter Emma, her best friend Faye, the town "weirdo" Mr. Henson all added that extra bulk to the story. Set in dual POVs (my favorite) we get clear picture of Lizzy and Tristan's grief and ensuing feelings for each other. <br><br><br><br>The first 80% of the book was clearly a five-star read for me. Then things started to deteriorate a bit. I have very little tolerance for immature drama (which is why I don't read much NA- but these MCs are in their early thirties). Drama I can take if it fits the character and the author stays true to that but with these two, revelations occur and they appeared to turn into two different people. Immature, selfish and heartless<s> to a little girl who's endured enough</s>. I also wasn't entirely in love with the whole suspenseful plot device towards the end. It just was a bit far-fetched and changed the whole tone of the book for me. But overall, I enjoyed this book and I look forward to more from Ms Cherry.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1398474043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8494888517083111333"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥ ♥ ♥ 4 STARS ♥ ♥ ♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443721848i/16399947._SY540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your loved one was remembering how to breathe.”<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440387869i/15969355._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I could not wait to read this book after seeing so many love it. I was hoping to feel the same, but I didn't fully love it as others. I did, however, enjoy it for the most part.<br/><br/>Elizabeth has had a very difficult year, to say the least. She lost her husband and has been trying t</span>
  <span id="freeText8494888517083111333" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥ ♥ ♥ 4 STARS ♥ ♥ ♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443721848i/16399947._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Sometimes the hardest part of existing without your loved one was remembering how to breathe.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440387869i/15969355._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I could not wait to read this book after seeing so many love it. I was hoping to feel the same, but I didn't fully love it as others. I did, however, enjoy it for the most part.<br><br>Elizabeth has had a very difficult year, to say the least. She lost her husband and has been trying to figure out how to cope with the grief. It's come to the point where she has to pull herself together for her five year old daughter's sake. So, she decides to go back to the small town where her life crumbled and live in the house she shared with her husband. This where she meets a strange and rude man who is actually her neighbour. His name is Tristan, and no matter what Elizabeth does to make this angry man a friend, he always has to act like a jerk. But, as days go on, it seems the share something in common. They are both struggling with the weight of their grief.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443722423ra/16399974.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Her soul was scarred, and mine was burned. <br>But when we were together, the hurting hurt a little less. When we were together, the past wasn’t as painful to take in. When we were together, I never for a second felt alone.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Tristan has lost his wife and his son, and has not been able to recover since it happened. The only person who seems to understand what he is going through is Elizabeth. He finds he is able to breathe easier and smile for the first time in months with Elizabeth and her daughter Emma in his life. That connection they share quickly turns into a hunger for their past. They want what they lost, and so, they use each other to pretend it was never gone. But soon, it becomes so much more. The attraction grows along with their feelings, to the point where they just want to be with each other and not the ghosts of their past.<br><br>The story itself, I felt flowed really well, and the way the relationship developed was at a really good pace. I liked the characters for the most part. Elizabeth I felt tried so hard and didn't want to give up on moving on even if it was painful. I liked that even though she was going through so much that she was able to be selfless and help this man with moving on as well. She was kind with him, and helped him slowly come back to himself. Tristan was such a big jerk at first. But you can see him change slowly throughout the book. They were both broken and they both helped each other try to put all their pieces back together. I loved watching their relationship grow, although the pretend part of their relationship I didn't really care for. It was just too weird to me. Thankfully it didn't last too long.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443722423ra/16399975.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book wasn't all sadness and tears, although I did feel and do that plenty of times while reading it. I was super happy to have some comic relief with my favourite character of the book, Faye, Elizabeth's best friend. She was blunt, hilarious, and just awesome. She had me laughing out loud many times. The writing was done really well, you could feel everything the characters were feeling. But near the end, I wasn't expecting things to turn so twisty. The first twist definitely got me and made things so much more interesting with a bit of angst. But the next one was so over the top. It was just so dramatic I didn't know if I was still reading the same book. The very end and epilogue however, left me very satisfied. I was very happy with how things concluded for them. Overall, it was a really great read. It wasn't perfect and I didn't completely love it, but there were many moments that were very enjoyable.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440387869i/15969355._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="8494888517083111333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1396870566" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1396870566" />
    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1396870566?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=br">br</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=h-o-t">h-o-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-fictional-boyfriends">my-fictional-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=cover-crush">cover-crush</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396870566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14756160442060690212"><b>***** 5 <i>Breathtaking</i> Stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by Author)<br/> (BR with Mel and Patty <3)</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/f15c19d2-c380-4454-8ed0-cea4a018d69c_zpsbrfyc7ay.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443023788i/16307786._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo f15c19d2-c380-4454-8ed0-cea4a018d69c_zpsbrfyc7ay.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When I first learned about this book, my first thought was, what a gorgeous cover! But what's inside the pages of this novel surpasses the attractive cover or any expectations I had about Brittainy C. Cherry's new book. <i>The Air He Breathes</i> is a thing of beauty, raw and emotional.<br/><br/>Elizabeth has been grieving the death of her husband. He died in a car accident a year ago and right after the funeral, she gra</span>
  <span id="freeText14756160442060690212" style="display:none"><b>***** 5 <i>Breathtaking</i> Stars*****</b><br><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by Author)<br> (BR with Mel and Patty &lt;3)</i><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/f15c19d2-c380-4454-8ed0-cea4a018d69c_zpsbrfyc7ay.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443023788i/16307786._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo f15c19d2-c380-4454-8ed0-cea4a018d69c_zpsbrfyc7ay.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I first learned about this book, my first thought was, what a gorgeous cover! But what's inside the pages of this novel surpasses the attractive cover or any expectations I had about Brittainy C. Cherry's new book. <i>The Air He Breathes</i> is a thing of beauty, raw and emotional.<br><br>Elizabeth has been grieving the death of her husband. He died in a car accident a year ago and right after the funeral, she grabbed her daughter and left town. She went to live with her mother because she needed distance between her and the home she shared with her husband. Being there without him was simply too painful for her. <br><br>Her relationship with her mother is not the best. Elizabeth doesn't approve of her mom's lifestyle. Ever since her father died her mom has been going from man to man looking for an answer to the loss. Fed-up with it, Elizabeth decides is time for her and her daughter Emma to go back home and face their new life.<br><br><br>Elizabeth has a new neighbor; Tristan Cole, a recluse that everybody claims is the new town crazy. When she comes face to face with him, she can see past his rugged and unkempt appearance. She can see her own soul in his eyes. She can see that they share the same pain, the same loss. <br><br><br>After a few explosive encounters, Tristan starts to realized that whenever Liz is around his numbness goes away. Whether it's annoyance or sexual tension, he feels. He no longer is a walking dead man when he is with her. Tristan and Liz start opening up about their pain. They've both lost loved ones and a big piece of themselves as well, and so they try to find refuge in each other. They find that they can both re-live their pasts through kisses and a fierce passion that while still painful, and makes them feel guilty, is the only thing that takes the loneliness away.<br><br><br><br>One day, they no longer see their dead spouses in each other. They only see and crave Tristan and Liz. The pain of the past has given them hope for the future. Tristan has fallen in love with Elizabeth and her daughter Emma. But just when things start looking up and they can finally see a light at the end of the tunnel a terrible secret threatens to take everything away, again.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"As long as air moves in and out of my lungs, as long as I breathe, I will fight for you. I will fight for us."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/b0e0ed69-8b6b-4af4-8d42-c05d993cd370_zpstpjujack.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443023788i/16307787.jpg" alt=" photo b0e0ed69-8b6b-4af4-8d42-c05d993cd370_zpstpjujack.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is one is one of those books you just want to hug tight. It was beautiful and heartbreaking but it also had a few moments where it made me laugh, hard. Every character in this story was complex and unique. Apart from loving Tristan and Liz; I adored her best friend Faye and Liz's daughter Emma, they added humor to the story. Even though this is a story mainly about grief and finding love after a big loss, it wasn't all sad. I've read a few books where grief is the main component in the plot and they make it all about the sadness and you even feel depressed after you read it, but not this one. Yes, it had sad moments but I found it so hopeful too. The message in this book was that love can heal, and that it's possible to love and do it hard even after a huge loss. Beautiful read, I loved it!<br><br>My <i>The Air He Breathes</i> music playlist:<br>*I Miss Her by Jessie J<br>*Babe I'm Gonna Leave You by Led Zeppellin<br>*Lover of The Light by Mumford and Sons<br>*One Day You Will by lady Antebellum<br>*Tomorrow by Avril Lavigne. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441511882i/16118321.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpsgbvgk2qi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

He knew what happened very well and he was in no way responsible, that was made very clear so why was he blaming himself? <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451545376ra/17557083.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Similar books? </b> Books where broken people fix each other!<br><br><b> Recommended :</b> Definitely, this book was awesome and really poignant. <br><br><b>Click On The Color Splashes To Join Me ;)</b><br><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer9307530817882510192"><u>5 Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day. ★'s</u><br/><br/><i>“You don’t have to be good all the time. It’s okay to be hurt sometimes. It’s okay to feel lost like you’re wandering around in the dark. It’s the bad days that make the good ones so much better.”</i><br/><br/>Wow! I mean damn this book, I love it!! It has all the feels, that for me is what makes a good book :) I love books with broken people, who learn to love again...in finding themselves in one another. It has such heartbreak and it's so raw. The Air </span>
  <span id="freeText9307530817882510192" style="display:none"><u>5 Every second. Every minute. Every hour. Every day. ★'s</u><br /><br /><i>“You don’t have to be good all the time. It’s okay to be hurt sometimes. It’s okay to feel lost like you’re wandering around in the dark. It’s the bad days that make the good ones so much better.”</i><br /><br />Wow! I mean damn this book, I love it!! It has all the feels, that for me is what makes a good book :) I love books with broken people, who learn to love again...in finding themselves in one another. It has such heartbreak and it's so raw. The Air He Breathes drew me in right way, from the very first sentence in the Prologue I was a goner. Hell Brittainy C. Cherry had put tears in my eyes within the first couple of chapters. I don't normally get all misty-eyed so early in a book but I love the way she writes and the way she tells a story. This is the very first book I have had the pleasure of reading by Brittainy and I do believe I will have a long-standing love here on out for her books. Okay, I think my review is good enough lol. This is keeping me from doing what I really gonna do and that is to check out the second book The Fire Between High &amp; Lo. <br /><br />♥By the way, that beautiful man on the cover is Franggy Yanez!♥ (sigh)<br /><br /><b>*Each book is a complete standalone with different characters.*</b></span>
