<div id="review_1384885653" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1384885653" />
    <a title="Olga therebelreader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24443337-olga-therebelreader"><img alt="Olga therebelreader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540920390p2/24443337.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1384885653?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Olga therebelreader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Olga therebelreader" href="/user/show/24443337-olga-therebelreader">Olga therebelreader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=tears">tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=suspense-angst">suspense-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24443337-olga-therebelreader?shelf=arc-cc-final-review">arc-cc-final-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1384885653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17876797800829458537">This story is so <b>beautifully-crafted!</b> I felt like I couldn’t read fast enough to know what would happen next. This was much more than just your typical romantic story. It was laugh, love, hurt, mystery all wrapped in one. The <u>force</u> in which the author writes about the inexplicable sorrow at having lost a wife or husband and a child is so intense and vivid.<br/><br/>It’s about two broken souls, Tristan and Elizabeth. Tristan lost his wife and 8 yr old son in a car accident about a year ago. Haunted by guil</span>
  <span id="freeText17876797800829458537" style="display:none">This story is so <b>beautifully-crafted!</b> I felt like I couldn’t read fast enough to know what would happen next. This was much more than just your typical romantic story. It was laugh, love, hurt, mystery all wrapped in one. The <u>force</u> in which the author writes about the inexplicable sorrow at having lost a wife or husband and a child is so intense and vivid.<br><br>It’s about two broken souls, Tristan and Elizabeth. Tristan lost his wife and 8 yr old son in a car accident about a year ago. Haunted by guilt, pain and sorrow, he left his house and family without a word and started anew in a different town. He now lives in isolation, his appearance is disheveled, he speaks little to people around him and the only thing he does is just work and mourn for those he’s lost. <br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/Olga_NNikolaidi/media/7533aaa5b03adc089b1b7889d623380a_zps1tejgnqy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442765467i/16276343._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7533aaa5b03adc089b1b7889d623380a_zps1tejgnqy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Elizabeth is a young woman who lost her husband a year ago and lives next to Tristan’s new house with her 5 yr old daughter, Emma. She has spiraled into a major depression, she’s living life in autopilot and only her lovely daughter helps her appreciate life. <br><br>Life’s games have sometimes unexpected twists and surprise us in the most weird way. This heart-wrenching and yet heart-warming story of two people who found love in darkness is absolutely powerful in its honesty and its true exploration of relationships, marriage and friendship. The author expertly guides us through this process whispering <b>hope</b> and <b>optimism</b>. <br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/Olga_NNikolaidi/media/abc8455c7678bee34feef0ade22d4168_zps2z5fjwoh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442765467i/16276344._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo abc8455c7678bee34feef0ade22d4168_zps2z5fjwoh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I recommend keeping some tissues close by, because shedding a few tears are more than likely. This story is chock full of <b>realism</b> and at times very <b>melancholic</b> and <b>gloomy</b>. The author gives us a poignant story, with secondary characters that add a little humor and sanity to a disheartening situation. <br><br>Life is full of coincidences, some very minor – but occasionally extraordinary. It’s unbelievable the power of coincidence and surprising connections all the time in our daily lives, yet we often fail to appreciate how they can guide us on our life’s path. This book explores how meaningful coincidence operates in our daily lives and intimate relationships. Truly spectacular!<br><br><i>ARC provided for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17876797800829458537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1396190088" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1396190088" />
    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1396190088?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=broken">broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=cry-me-a-river">cry-me-a-river</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1396190088" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer239941358722112392"><b>4.5 "Because I see you" STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"There were small signs from the angels, letting us know they were always close by, watching over us."</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/ZxCznDt' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443567914ra/16377332.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>I truly love discovering a new author and then falling in love with their characters and story. Thank you, Ms. Cherry! <b>You made me smile, you made me laugh, you made me cry and Tristan, Elizabeth, Emma and Zeus stole my heart.</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/image.jpg1_zpskjc1hehu.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443567914i/16377333._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg1_zpskjc1hehu.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was a beautiful, breathtaking read with so many emotions. It covers the very harsh and dreadful reality of death, grief and </span>
  <span id="freeText239941358722112392" style="display:none"><b>4.5 "Because I see you" STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"There were small signs from the angels, letting us know they were always close by, watching over us."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/ZxCznDt" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443567914ra/16377332.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>I truly love discovering a new author and then falling in love with their characters and story. Thank you, Ms. Cherry! <b>You made me smile, you made me laugh, you made me cry and Tristan, Elizabeth, Emma and Zeus stole my heart.</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/image.jpg1_zpskjc1hehu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443567914i/16377333._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpskjc1hehu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was a beautiful, breathtaking read with so many emotions. It covers the very harsh and dreadful reality of death, grief and loss of your partner, your child and your life as you know it. <br><br>Ms. Cherry did a brilliant job of creating such vibrant, broken and life-like characters that made this story so deep and moving. We all grieve differently and there is no right and wrong. This story is all about that and how two shattered souls find a way to make their broken pieces fit.<br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/image.jpg6_zpskog8x7rd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443567914i/16377334._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg6_zpskog8x7rd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"Show me the shadows that keep you up at night. Kiss me with your darkness."<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/iqjJlke" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441888698ra/16165431.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>"She undressed me and made love to her past. I slid into her and made love to my ghosts."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/JSrj3qw" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443567914ra/16377335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would have given this 5 stars but two things jarred me. Towards the last 20% of the book, the pace picked up to the point that it felt rushed (up until then it had been a slow and measured build) and drama ensued that seemed out of nowhere. Sure, there were some very minor clues in retrospect but there was no indication it was going in that direction. But needless to say, this was not big enough to kill the aura and beauty of this tale.<br><br><b>I would highly recommend this book to anyone who wants a story to move them, empty them and then fill them up again in the best way possible!</b> <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/5m0Zrfl" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443567914ra/16377336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b><br><br> <a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17246896051855894367">3 Stars!<br/>Loved the first half of the book. It's the last part that I had issues with. <br/>Review posted:)<br/>3 Loved/Liked Stars!<br/>This one started out really good. I was loving it so much. I didn't want to put it down. Then a few things happened that brought my loving down to just liking. <br/><br/>What did I love?<br/>I loved Faye! She was funny as hell!<br/>I loved Emma...Elizabeth's daughter. <br/>Her calling Tristan a Tick was cute and funny. <br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I loved that Tristan bought thousands of white feathers for Emma to k</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17246896051855894367" style="display:none">3 Stars!<br />Loved the first half of the book. It's the last part that I had issues with. <br />Review posted:)<br />3 Loved/Liked Stars!<br />This one started out really good. I was loving it so much. I didn't want to put it down. Then a few things happened that brought my loving down to just liking. <br /><br />What did I love?<br />I loved Faye! She was funny as hell!<br />I loved Emma...Elizabeth's daughter. <br />Her calling Tristan a Tick was cute and funny. <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I loved that Tristan bought thousands of white feathers for Emma to keep her from freaking out about her father. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />I thought Mr Henson was awesome. <br />Tristan having his sons favorite books tattooed on him was different and I loved that too. <br />Tristan's past choked me up. I may have had very watery eyes reading about his loss. <br />I loved Tristan! <br />There were moments that Elizabeth and Tristan were together that I loved. <br /><br />What didn't work for me?<br />I didn't like how Tristan and Elizabeth used each other at first. <br />I didn't like that Emma seemed to always be at her grandparents or just away. <br />I didn't like that I figured out what was going to cause issues between Tristan and Elizabeth later on. <br /><br />But regardless of the things that weren't working for me I was still enjoying the book for the most part. Then at 70% I was saying I knew that was coming. At 80% I was still saying to myself that I knew that was going to happen also. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was sort of disappointed in Elizabeth at how instead of telling Tristan about what Tanner told her she decides to have sex with Tristan and finally tell him she loved him. She decides to start cleaning out Stevens clothes also. Ugh! So that made me say...well Tanner is going to tell Tristan and it's going to be ugly! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />I was still ready to slap 4 stars on this baby though. <br />*****Might be spoilerish below!*****<br />Now what made me want to skim to the end was all the drama with Tanner. I'm just not really sure why all of that had to happen. It pretty much ruined the book for me. It was way OTT! I almost wish I would of quit reading at 80% and skipped to the epilogue. lol <br /><br />With that being said. I love this author and still have other books of hers that I need to get to. But even though I loved most of this book I also had many issues with it as well so that's why it gets 3 Stars from me which means that I liked it:))</span>

<div id="review_1403579176" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1403579176" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1403579176?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1403579176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1899692192147023211"><b>Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 1 of Elements series<br/><b>POV: </b> First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423545558i/13641856.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443676937i/16394347.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Tristan Cole was a broken man still haunted by the memories of the past. He stopped feeling and living for himself, earning him a reputation and making him an outcast of the small town.<br/><br/>Elizabeth Bailey came back to her hometown for a fresh start. Together with her 5 years old daughter, she vowed to move on with their life with beautiful new memories. But sometimes, the past could creep in une</span>
  <span id="freeText1899692192147023211" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 1 of Elements series<br><b>POV: </b> First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423545558i/13641856.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443676937i/16394347.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tristan Cole was a broken man still haunted by the memories of the past. He stopped feeling and living for himself, earning him a reputation and making him an outcast of the small town.<br><br>Elizabeth Bailey came back to her hometown for a fresh start. Together with her 5 years old daughter, she vowed to move on with their life with beautiful new memories. But sometimes, the past could creep in unexpectedly. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This book has been blowing up my GR feed for days with the stellar reviews and the promise of tears, it was too tempting to ignore. This was my first book of the author and from the look of it, would not be the last.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I’d seen the harsh realities that lived in Tristan. But I’d also seen another side of him that many didn’t notice.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Broken heroes will always be my favorite and Tristan was as broken as one could get. He was incredibly vulnerable and I could feel his pain and understood why he was as cold and abrasive towards others.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443677271i/16394464.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how Liz brought happiness into his life even when she had her own pain to deal with. I like seeing how strong she was for her willingness to face the past and take chances for the future.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>She undressed me and made love to her past. I slid into her and made love to my ghosts.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I like seeing them together bonded by grief, just trying to live day by day. But there were point where I felt so sad for who they were to each other because they were being incredibly unfair not only to each other but to themselves.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443676908i/16394341.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though I didn’t find the book as heartbreaking as I wanted it to be, it was sad enough to meet my need of emotional pain. I supposed because their pain was related to the past than the present, made me felt it less. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“When does life stop hurting?” <br>“When we learn to tell life to fuck off and we find the littlest reasons to smile.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The book had a gloomy feel like a dark damp winter morning, but broken up by rays of light in between. One of them was her straight talking best friend Faye. And Tick and Tock absolutely melted by cold heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“No! He never takes this long! There’s no feathers! We have to go back!”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>One of the best thing in the book for me was the feathers and the best scene was the morning surprise. Every time there was a scene involving feathers I felt like my heart being stabbed. <br><br>Even though the story was predictable, I do like it overall. After the slower pace of the earlier part, at times I felt like the ending was packed with too much within a short period of time and too… perfect/sweet for my personal liking.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It’s okay to be hurt sometimes. It’s okay to feel lost like you’re wandering around in the dark. It’s the bad days that make the good ones so much better.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The Air He Breathes is a story about two broken people bound by their past working towards a meaningful future.<br><br> <i><b>Note: </b><br>I like that the book feather theme matched my blog theme, except mine is less innocent lol! </i><br><br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412943984i/11445453.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415355089i/11776478.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/WarhawkesVault" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415355222i/11776486.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/warhawkestudios" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415355222i/11776487.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/warhawkesvault/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420280057i/13200248.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.tsu.co/WarhawkesVault" rel="nofollow noopener">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CrXcUycWS2qSDLavaO9Ukk+W3NcyMuk4d7p1L3YoCzSngML94wdretLCYVzMqieJ7hu4sxGQNN7gC0rywnbGvA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LxVYF3zBTGyufcG1O6Hc31WZeA+pppayTsA/tpKguCKCIEa5uNBsfO6zFkaf5K/E9BQca4oES1TZcQBrJv51qg==')})
  }
//]]>
